function fireEventOnField(eventName,fieldObj){
		if(!fieldObj) return;
		if(fieldObj.dispatchEvent){
			var customevent = document.createEvent("HTMLEvents");
			customevent.initEvent(eventName,true,false);
			fieldObj.dispatchEvent(customevent);
		}else if(fieldObj.fireEvent){
			fieldObj.fireEvent("on"+eventName);
		}
}

var tempObj;
if((tempObj=document.getElementById("pyRangeFiltering"))){
	if(tempObj.value.indexOf("pyCustomerID")!=-1){
		tempObj.value="";
	}
}

/*Grid related JS code (will be executed only once)*/
if(!document.getElementById("grid_openRuleAdvanced_jsLoaded")){
	var isGridPropertyPanel=false;
	var gridlRuleSet="";
	var gridlRuleSetVersion="";
	var gridsectionClassName="";
	var gridrowPageClassName="";
	if(document.getElementById("pySourceType") && document.getElementById("pyRowVisible")){
		isGridPropertyPanel=true;
	}
	if(isGridPropertyPanel){
	
		/*START: reading info from pagesAndClassesTab*/
		var inputList=document.getElementsByTagName("input");
		var pagesList=[];
		var classesList=[];
		for(var i=0;i<inputList.length;i++){
			if(inputList[i].id=="pyPagesAndClassesPage"){
				pagesList.push(inputList[i].value);
			}else if(inputList[i].id=="pyPagesAndClassesClass"){
				classesList.push(inputList[i].value);
			}
		}
		/*END: reading info from pagesAndClassesTab*/
		
		/*reading PRXML from section xml for getting info about PagesAndClasses and Section Parameters*/
		if(document.getElementById("PRXML")){
			var txt=document.getElementById("PRXML").value;
			txt=txt.replace(/\n[ ]*/g, "");
			if(txt.trim){
				txt=txt.trim();
			}
			var cache_prxml=window.cachedPRXML;
			if(!cache_prxml){cache_prxml="";}
			cache_prxml=cache_prxml.replace(/\n[ ]*/g, "");
			if(cache_prxml.trim){
				cache_prxml=cache_prxml.trim();
			}
			var xmlDoc=pega.tools.XMLDocument.get();
			xmlDoc.async= false;
			xmlDoc.loadXML(txt); 
			var xmlDocCache=pega.tools.XMLDocument.get();
			xmlDocCache.async= false;
			xmlDocCache.loadXML(cache_prxml); 
			try{
				gridsectionClassName=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyClassName")[0].text;
			}catch(sectionClassNotFoundError){
				try{
					gridsectionClassName=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyClassName")[0].text;
				}catch(promptClassNotFoundError){
					try{gridsectionClassName=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyPromptClass")[0].text;}catch(err){}
				}
			}
			setTimeout(function(){
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridsectionClassName;
						fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			},1250);
			try{
				gridlRuleSet=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSet")[0].text;
			}catch(err){
				try{gridlRuleSet=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSet")[0].text;}catch(err1){}
			}
			try{
				gridlRuleSetVersion=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSetVersion")[0].text;
			}catch(err){
				try{gridlRuleSetVersion=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSetVersion")[0].text;}catch(err2){}
			}
			var pagesAndClasses;
			try{
				pagesAndClasses=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClasses")[0];
				if(!pagesAndClasses){
					pagesAndClasses=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClasses")[0];
				}
			}catch(err){
			}
			var sectionparameters;
			try{
				sectionparameters=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyParameters")[0];
				if(!sectionparameters){
					sectionparameters=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyParameters")[0];
				}
			}catch(err){
			}
			if(pagesAndClasses){
			var allpages=pagesAndClasses.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClassesPage");
			var allclasses=pagesAndClasses.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClassesClass");
			}
			try{
				/*storing the xml version as text for consumption in pzExpressionBuilderGadget*/
				var gridsectionparameters_txt=sectionparameters.xml;
			}catch(err){
				var gridsectionparameters_txt="";
			}
			try{
				/*storing the xml version as text for consumption in pzExpressionBuilderGadget*/
				var gridsectionpagesandclasses_txt=pagesAndClasses.xml;
			}catch(err){
				var gridsectionpagesandclasses_txt="";
			}
			
		}
		
		if(document.getElementById("pySourceType")){
			/*Tried using "Run Script", but it did not work, so manually registering the change listener*/
			pega.util.Event.addListener(document.getElementById("pySourceType"),"change", setFocusOnDSField);
			var sourceTypeField=document.getElementById("pySourceType");
			var sourceFieldValue=sourceTypeField[sourceTypeField.selectedIndex].value;
			if(sourceFieldValue=="Property"){
				/*emptying the pyPageListProperty field on UI when the value is .pyTemplatePageList -> when dropping a new grid */
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty") && document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty").value.indexOf("pyTemplatePagelist")!=-1){
					document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty").value="";
				}
				/*Updating the rowpageclass variable*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
			}else if(sourceFieldValue=="Report Definition"){
				/*Update gridrowclass variable*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyRDAppliesTo")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyRDAppliesTo").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
				/*Wait for DOM to be ready after Refresh Section happens.*/
				/*setTimeout(function(){setRDPageDefaults();},1000);*/
			}else if(sourceFieldValue=="Data Object"){
				/*Update rowpageclass*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyDPResultsClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyDPResultsClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
			}
			/*updating the "PrevValue" with current selection.*/
			document.getElementById("pySourceType").setAttribute("PrevValue",sourceFieldValue);
		}
		/*creating a hidden DOM element to ensure that code is executed only once.*/
		var jsLoadedIndicator=document.createElement("div");
		jsLoadedIndicator.id="grid_openRuleAdvanced_jsLoaded";
		jsLoadedIndicator.style.display="none";
		document.getElementById("pySourceType").parentNode.appendChild(jsLoadedIndicator);
	}
}

var gridFieldPromptingMappings={
"pyActivity":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120548*/,
"pyProperty":"ROWCLASS",
"pyDataSource":"ROWCLASS" /*DISPLAY->MENU*/,
"pyRowRefreshIndex":"ROWCLASS",
"pyActivityClass":"ROWCLASS",
"pySelectedFlowAction":"ROWCLASS" /*PROCESS WORK->PERFORM ACTION*/,
"pyLocalAction":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120596 Launch -> Local Action -> with / without using page */,
"pyWindowName":"ROWCLASS",
"pyValue":"ROWCLASS",
"pyClipboardPage":"ROWCLASS",
"pyWhen":"ROWCLASS",
"pyElementName":"ROWCLASS",
"pyName":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120599, BUG-120548*/,
"pyCategoryHeaderTemplate":"ROWCLASS",
"pyInsName":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120538*/,
"pyInsKey":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120524*/,
"pySelectedFlow":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120590*/,
"pyHarnessName":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120593*/,
"pyKey":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120524*/,
"pyItemId":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120524*/
};

if(!gridFieldPromptingMappings.checkAndUpdatePrompting){
	gridFieldPromptingMappings.checkAndUpdatePrompting=function(fieldObj){
		if(!(document.getElementById("pySourceType") && document.getElementById("pyRowVisible"))){
			return; /*This API is intended only for Repeating Grids, Tree, TreeGrids hence returning from here in other cases. Please do not alter this logic.*/
		}
		if(!fieldObj){return;}
		if(this[fieldObj.id]=="ROWCLASS"){
			if(fieldObj.getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS")){
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(fieldObj.getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			}
		}else if(this[fieldObj.id]=="CUSTOMHANDLING"){
			try{
				GridPropertyPanelActionMappings["handle_"+fieldObj.id]();
				/*Function("GridPropertyPanelActionMappings.handle_"+fieldObj.id+"();")();*/
			}catch(err){
				if(window.console && window.console.log){window.console.log("Error: "+err);}
			}
		}
	};
}

window.GridPropertyPanelActionMappings={
	handle_pyHarnessName:function(){ /*BUG-120593*/ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
	var tmp;
		if((tmp=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass")) && tmp.value==""){
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyHarnessName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pySelectedFlow:function(){ /*BUG-120590*/ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value!=""){
			var pySelectedFlowPromptClass="";
			if(pagesList.length>0 && classesList.length>0){
				for(var q=0;q<pagesList.length;q++){
					if(pagesList[q]==document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value){
						pySelectedFlowPromptClass=classesList[q];
					}
				}
			}
			if(pySelectedFlowPromptClass!=""){
					var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pySelectedFlow").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
					for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
						promptFields[i].value=pySelectedFlowPromptClass;
					}
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
						document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=pySelectedFlowPromptClass;
						fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
					}		
			}
		}else if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value==""){
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pySelectedFlow").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pyActivity:function(){ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyTarget") && document.getElementById("pyTarget")[document.getElementById("pyTarget").selectedIndex].value=="otherSection"){
			this.handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction();
		}else{
			var activityPromptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyActivity").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<activityPromptFields.length;i++){
				activityPromptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pyName:function(){ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyTarget") && document.getElementById("pyTarget")[document.getElementById("pyTarget").selectedIndex].value=="otherSection"){
			this.handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction();
		}else{
			/*BUG-120599: For Report Definition nothing has to be done, but only in case of Open URL in Window (Rule-Obj-Model) some logic is required.*/ 
			/*BUG-120585: Case of Set Value (Rule-Obj-Property) */
			if(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("isns_class")=="Rule-Obj-Model" || document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("isns_class")=="Rule-Obj-Property"){ /*case of Open URL in Window*/
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			}
		}
	},
	handle_pyLocalAction:function(){ /*BUG-120596: Handling Local Action with & without "using page" */ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value==""){ /*without using page -> prompt from row class*/
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyLocalAction").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}
		}else if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value!=""){ /*with using page -> prompt from page class / user entered input class */
			if(!document.getElementById("pyClass") || document.getElementById("pyClass").value==""){
				return;
			}
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyLocalAction").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyClass").value;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=document.getElementById("pyClass").value;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction:function(){ /*Called from within handle_pyActivity, handle_pyName*/
		if(!document.getElementById("pyTarget")){
			return;
		}
		var pyTargetDropDown=document.getElementById("pyTarget");
		var selval=pyTargetDropDown[pyTargetDropDown.selectedIndex].value;
		if(selval=="otherSection"){
			if(document.getElementById("pyActivityClass") && document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value!=""){
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
				}
				var activityPromptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyActivity").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<activityPromptFields.length;i++){
					activityPromptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}		
			}
		}
	}
};

function onChangeHandler(elem, event){
	var evt = window.event || event;
	var srcElement = evt.srcElement || evt.target;
	if(srcElement === elem){
		if(!OpenRuleAdvanced_isActive()) { 
			if(elem.getAttribute("ONCHANGE_CUSTOM") != null) {
				eval(elem.getAttribute("ONCHANGE_CUSTOM"));
			}
			if(elem.getAttribute("ONBLUR_CUSTOM") !=null) {
				eval(elem.getAttribute("ONBLUR_CUSTOM"));
			}
		} 
	}
	else{
		pega.util.Event.fireEvent(elem,'onchange');
		pega.util.Event.fireEvent(elem,'onblur');
	}
}
</script>

	function SmartPromptFocusHandler(e) {
		var evt = e || window.event || arguments.callee.caller.arguments[0];
 		if(typeof(evt)  != "undefined" ) {
			var evtTarget = evt.srcElement || evt.target;
			if (ISnsSmartPromptInitActive(evtTarget, false))
				return;
		}		
	}
	function zUtil_SmartPromptFocusHandler(e) {
		var evt = e || window.event || arguments.callee.caller.arguments[0];
		SmartPromptFocusHandler(evt);
	}

<script>

  


function fireEventOnField(eventName,fieldObj){
		if(!fieldObj) return;
		if(fieldObj.dispatchEvent){
			var customevent = document.createEvent("HTMLEvents");
			customevent.initEvent(eventName,true,false);
			fieldObj.dispatchEvent(customevent);
		}else if(fieldObj.fireEvent){
			fieldObj.fireEvent("on"+eventName);
		}
}

var tempObj;
if((tempObj=document.getElementById("pyRangeFiltering"))){
	if(tempObj.value.indexOf("pyCustomerID")!=-1){
		tempObj.value="";
	}
}

/*Grid related JS code (will be executed only once)*/
if(!document.getElementById("grid_openRuleAdvanced_jsLoaded")){
	var isGridPropertyPanel=false;
	var gridlRuleSet="";
	var gridlRuleSetVersion="";
	var gridsectionClassName="";
	var gridrowPageClassName="";
	if(document.getElementById("pySourceType") && document.getElementById("pyRowVisible")){
		isGridPropertyPanel=true;
	}
	if(isGridPropertyPanel){
	
		/*START: reading info from pagesAndClassesTab*/
		var inputList=document.getElementsByTagName("input");
		var pagesList=[];
		var classesList=[];
		for(var i=0;i<inputList.length;i++){
			if(inputList[i].id=="pyPagesAndClassesPage"){
				pagesList.push(inputList[i].value);
			}else if(inputList[i].id=="pyPagesAndClassesClass"){
				classesList.push(inputList[i].value);
			}
		}
		/*END: reading info from pagesAndClassesTab*/
		
		/*reading PRXML from section xml for getting info about PagesAndClasses and Section Parameters*/
		if(document.getElementById("PRXML")){
			var txt=document.getElementById("PRXML").value;
			txt=txt.replace(/\n[ ]*/g, "");
			if(txt.trim){
				txt=txt.trim();
			}
			var cache_prxml=window.cachedPRXML;
			if(!cache_prxml){cache_prxml="";}
			cache_prxml=cache_prxml.replace(/\n[ ]*/g, "");
			if(cache_prxml.trim){
				cache_prxml=cache_prxml.trim();
			}
			var xmlDoc=pega.tools.XMLDocument.get();
			xmlDoc.async= false;
			xmlDoc.loadXML(txt); 
			var xmlDocCache=pega.tools.XMLDocument.get();
			xmlDocCache.async= false;
			xmlDocCache.loadXML(cache_prxml); 
			try{
				gridsectionClassName=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyClassName")[0].text;
			}catch(sectionClassNotFoundError){
				try{
					gridsectionClassName=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyClassName")[0].text;
				}catch(promptClassNotFoundError){
					try{gridsectionClassName=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyPromptClass")[0].text;}catch(err){}
				}
			}
			setTimeout(function(){
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridsectionClassName;
						fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			},1250);
			try{
				gridlRuleSet=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSet")[0].text;
			}catch(err){
				try{gridlRuleSet=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSet")[0].text;}catch(err1){}
			}
			try{
				gridlRuleSetVersion=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSetVersion")[0].text;
			}catch(err){
				try{gridlRuleSetVersion=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSetVersion")[0].text;}catch(err2){}
			}
			var pagesAndClasses;
			try{
				pagesAndClasses=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClasses")[0];
				if(!pagesAndClasses){
					pagesAndClasses=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClasses")[0];
				}
			}catch(err){
			}
			var sectionparameters;
			try{
				sectionparameters=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyParameters")[0];
				if(!sectionparameters){
					sectionparameters=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyParameters")[0];
				}
			}catch(err){
			}
			if(pagesAndClasses){
			var allpages=pagesAndClasses.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClassesPage");
			var allclasses=pagesAndClasses.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClassesClass");
			}
			try{
				/*storing the xml version as text for consumption in pzExpressionBuilderGadget*/
				var gridsectionparameters_txt=sectionparameters.xml;
			}catch(err){
				var gridsectionparameters_txt="";
			}
			try{
				/*storing the xml version as text for consumption in pzExpressionBuilderGadget*/
				var gridsectionpagesandclasses_txt=pagesAndClasses.xml;
			}catch(err){
				var gridsectionpagesandclasses_txt="";
			}
			
		}
		
		if(document.getElementById("pySourceType")){
			/*Tried using "Run Script", but it did not work, so manually registering the change listener*/
			pega.util.Event.addListener(document.getElementById("pySourceType"),"change", setFocusOnDSField);
			var sourceTypeField=document.getElementById("pySourceType");
			var sourceFieldValue=sourceTypeField[sourceTypeField.selectedIndex].value;
			if(sourceFieldValue=="Property"){
				/*emptying the pyPageListProperty field on UI when the value is .pyTemplatePageList -> when dropping a new grid */
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty") && document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty").value.indexOf("pyTemplatePagelist")!=-1){
					document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty").value="";
				}
				/*Updating the rowpageclass variable*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
			}else if(sourceFieldValue=="Report Definition"){
				/*Update gridrowclass variable*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyRDAppliesTo")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyRDAppliesTo").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
				/*Wait for DOM to be ready after Refresh Section happens.*/
				/*setTimeout(function(){setRDPageDefaults();},1000);*/
			}else if(sourceFieldValue=="Data Object"){
				/*Update rowpageclass*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyDPResultsClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyDPResultsClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
			}
			/*updating the "PrevValue" with current selection.*/
			document.getElementById("pySourceType").setAttribute("PrevValue",sourceFieldValue);
		}
		/*creating a hidden DOM element to ensure that code is executed only once.*/
		var jsLoadedIndicator=document.createElement("div");
		jsLoadedIndicator.id="grid_openRuleAdvanced_jsLoaded";
		jsLoadedIndicator.style.display="none";
		document.getElementById("pySourceType").parentNode.appendChild(jsLoadedIndicator);
	}
}

var gridFieldPromptingMappings={
"pyActivity":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120548*/,
"pyProperty":"ROWCLASS",
"pyDataSource":"ROWCLASS" /*DISPLAY->MENU*/,
"pyRowRefreshIndex":"ROWCLASS",
"pyActivityClass":"ROWCLASS",
"pySelectedFlowAction":"ROWCLASS" /*PROCESS WORK->PERFORM ACTION*/,
"pyLocalAction":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120596 Launch -> Local Action -> with / without using page */,
"pyWindowName":"ROWCLASS",
"pyValue":"ROWCLASS",
"pyClipboardPage":"ROWCLASS",
"pyWhen":"ROWCLASS",
"pyElementName":"ROWCLASS",
"pyName":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120599, BUG-120548*/,
"pyCategoryHeaderTemplate":"ROWCLASS",
"pyInsName":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120538*/,
"pyInsKey":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120524*/,
"pySelectedFlow":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120590*/,
"pyHarnessName":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120593*/,
"pyKey":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120524*/,
"pyItemId":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120524*/
};

if(!gridFieldPromptingMappings.checkAndUpdatePrompting){
	gridFieldPromptingMappings.checkAndUpdatePrompting=function(fieldObj){
		if(!(document.getElementById("pySourceType") && document.getElementById("pyRowVisible"))){
			return; /*This API is intended only for Repeating Grids, Tree, TreeGrids hence returning from here in other cases. Please do not alter this logic.*/
		}
		if(!fieldObj){return;}
		if(this[fieldObj.id]=="ROWCLASS"){
			if(fieldObj.getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS")){
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(fieldObj.getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			}
		}else if(this[fieldObj.id]=="CUSTOMHANDLING"){
			try{
				GridPropertyPanelActionMappings["handle_"+fieldObj.id]();
				/*Function("GridPropertyPanelActionMappings.handle_"+fieldObj.id+"();")();*/
			}catch(err){
				if(window.console && window.console.log){window.console.log("Error: "+err);}
			}
		}
	};
}

window.GridPropertyPanelActionMappings={
	handle_pyHarnessName:function(){ /*BUG-120593*/ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
	var tmp;
		if((tmp=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass")) && tmp.value==""){
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyHarnessName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pySelectedFlow:function(){ /*BUG-120590*/ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value!=""){
			var pySelectedFlowPromptClass="";
			if(pagesList.length>0 && classesList.length>0){
				for(var q=0;q<pagesList.length;q++){
					if(pagesList[q]==document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value){
						pySelectedFlowPromptClass=classesList[q];
					}
				}
			}
			if(pySelectedFlowPromptClass!=""){
					var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pySelectedFlow").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
					for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
						promptFields[i].value=pySelectedFlowPromptClass;
					}
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
						document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=pySelectedFlowPromptClass;
						fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
					}		
			}
		}else if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value==""){
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pySelectedFlow").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pyActivity:function(){ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyTarget") && document.getElementById("pyTarget")[document.getElementById("pyTarget").selectedIndex].value=="otherSection"){
			this.handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction();
		}else{
			var activityPromptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyActivity").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<activityPromptFields.length;i++){
				activityPromptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pyName:function(){ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyTarget") && document.getElementById("pyTarget")[document.getElementById("pyTarget").selectedIndex].value=="otherSection"){
			this.handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction();
		}else{
			/*BUG-120599: For Report Definition nothing has to be done, but only in case of Open URL in Window (Rule-Obj-Model) some logic is required.*/ 
			/*BUG-120585: Case of Set Value (Rule-Obj-Property) */
			if(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("isns_class")=="Rule-Obj-Model" || document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("isns_class")=="Rule-Obj-Property"){ /*case of Open URL in Window*/
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			}
		}
	},
	handle_pyLocalAction:function(){ /*BUG-120596: Handling Local Action with & without "using page" */ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value==""){ /*without using page -> prompt from row class*/
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyLocalAction").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}
		}else if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value!=""){ /*with using page -> prompt from page class / user entered input class */
			if(!document.getElementById("pyClass") || document.getElementById("pyClass").value==""){
				return;
			}
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyLocalAction").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyClass").value;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=document.getElementById("pyClass").value;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction:function(){ /*Called from within handle_pyActivity, handle_pyName*/
		if(!document.getElementById("pyTarget")){
			return;
		}
		var pyTargetDropDown=document.getElementById("pyTarget");
		var selval=pyTargetDropDown[pyTargetDropDown.selectedIndex].value;
		if(selval=="otherSection"){
			if(document.getElementById("pyActivityClass") && document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value!=""){
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
				}
				var activityPromptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyActivity").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<activityPromptFields.length;i++){
					activityPromptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}		
			}
		}
	}
};

function onChangeHandler(elem, event){
	var evt = window.event || event;
	var srcElement = evt.srcElement || evt.target;
	if(srcElement === elem){
		if(!OpenRuleAdvanced_isActive()) { 
			if(elem.getAttribute("ONCHANGE_CUSTOM") != null) {
				eval(elem.getAttribute("ONCHANGE_CUSTOM"));
			}
			if(elem.getAttribute("ONBLUR_CUSTOM") !=null) {
				eval(elem.getAttribute("ONBLUR_CUSTOM"));
			}
		} 
	}
	else{
		pega.util.Event.fireEvent(elem,'onchange');
		pega.util.Event.fireEvent(elem,'onblur');
	}
}

function fireEventOnField(eventName,fieldObj){
		if(!fieldObj) return;
		if(fieldObj.dispatchEvent){
			var customevent = document.createEvent("HTMLEvents");
			customevent.initEvent(eventName,true,false);
			fieldObj.dispatchEvent(customevent);
		}else if(fieldObj.fireEvent){
			fieldObj.fireEvent("on"+eventName);
		}
}

var tempObj;
if((tempObj=document.getElementById("pyRangeFiltering"))){
	if(tempObj.value.indexOf("pyCustomerID")!=-1){
		tempObj.value="";
	}
}

/*Grid related JS code (will be executed only once)*/
if(!document.getElementById("grid_openRuleAdvanced_jsLoaded")){
	var isGridPropertyPanel=false;
	var gridlRuleSet="";
	var gridlRuleSetVersion="";
	var gridsectionClassName="";
	var gridrowPageClassName="";
	if(document.getElementById("pySourceType") && document.getElementById("pyRowVisible")){
		isGridPropertyPanel=true;
	}
	if(isGridPropertyPanel){
	
		/*START: reading info from pagesAndClassesTab*/
		var inputList=document.getElementsByTagName("input");
		var pagesList=[];
		var classesList=[];
		for(var i=0;i<inputList.length;i++){
			if(inputList[i].id=="pyPagesAndClassesPage"){
				pagesList.push(inputList[i].value);
			}else if(inputList[i].id=="pyPagesAndClassesClass"){
				classesList.push(inputList[i].value);
			}
		}
		/*END: reading info from pagesAndClassesTab*/
		
		/*reading PRXML from section xml for getting info about PagesAndClasses and Section Parameters*/
		if(document.getElementById("PRXML")){
			var txt=document.getElementById("PRXML").value;
			txt=txt.replace(/\n[ ]*/g, "");
			if(txt.trim){
				txt=txt.trim();
			}
			var cache_prxml=window.cachedPRXML;
			if(!cache_prxml){cache_prxml="";}
			cache_prxml=cache_prxml.replace(/\n[ ]*/g, "");
			if(cache_prxml.trim){
				cache_prxml=cache_prxml.trim();
			}
			var xmlDoc=pega.tools.XMLDocument.get();
			xmlDoc.async= false;
			xmlDoc.loadXML(txt); 
			var xmlDocCache=pega.tools.XMLDocument.get();
			xmlDocCache.async= false;
			xmlDocCache.loadXML(cache_prxml); 
			try{
				gridsectionClassName=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyClassName")[0].text;
			}catch(sectionClassNotFoundError){
				try{
					gridsectionClassName=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyClassName")[0].text;
				}catch(promptClassNotFoundError){
					try{gridsectionClassName=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyPromptClass")[0].text;}catch(err){}
				}
			}
			setTimeout(function(){
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridsectionClassName;
						fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			},1250);
			try{
				gridlRuleSet=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSet")[0].text;
			}catch(err){
				try{gridlRuleSet=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSet")[0].text;}catch(err1){}
			}
			try{
				gridlRuleSetVersion=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSetVersion")[0].text;
			}catch(err){
				try{gridlRuleSetVersion=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSetVersion")[0].text;}catch(err2){}
			}
			var pagesAndClasses;
			try{
				pagesAndClasses=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClasses")[0];
				if(!pagesAndClasses){
					pagesAndClasses=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClasses")[0];
				}
			}catch(err){
			}
			var sectionparameters;
			try{
				sectionparameters=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyParameters")[0];
				if(!sectionparameters){
					sectionparameters=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyParameters")[0];
				}
			}catch(err){
			}
			if(pagesAndClasses){
			var allpages=pagesAndClasses.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClassesPage");
			var allclasses=pagesAndClasses.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClassesClass");
			}
			try{
				/*storing the xml version as text for consumption in pzExpressionBuilderGadget*/
				var gridsectionparameters_txt=sectionparameters.xml;
			}catch(err){
				var gridsectionparameters_txt="";
			}
			try{
				/*storing the xml version as text for consumption in pzExpressionBuilderGadget*/
				var gridsectionpagesandclasses_txt=pagesAndClasses.xml;
			}catch(err){
				var gridsectionpagesandclasses_txt="";
			}
			
		}
		
		if(document.getElementById("pySourceType")){
			/*Tried using "Run Script", but it did not work, so manually registering the change listener*/
			pega.util.Event.addListener(document.getElementById("pySourceType"),"change", setFocusOnDSField);
			var sourceTypeField=document.getElementById("pySourceType");
			var sourceFieldValue=sourceTypeField[sourceTypeField.selectedIndex].value;
			if(sourceFieldValue=="Property"){
				/*emptying the pyPageListProperty field on UI when the value is .pyTemplatePageList -> when dropping a new grid */
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty") && document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty").value.indexOf("pyTemplatePagelist")!=-1){
					document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty").value="";
				}
				/*Updating the rowpageclass variable*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
			}else if(sourceFieldValue=="Report Definition"){
				/*Update gridrowclass variable*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyRDAppliesTo")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyRDAppliesTo").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
				/*Wait for DOM to be ready after Refresh Section happens.*/
				/*setTimeout(function(){setRDPageDefaults();},1000);*/
			}else if(sourceFieldValue=="Data Object"){
				/*Update rowpageclass*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyDPResultsClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyDPResultsClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
			}
			/*updating the "PrevValue" with current selection.*/
			document.getElementById("pySourceType").setAttribute("PrevValue",sourceFieldValue);
		}
		/*creating a hidden DOM element to ensure that code is executed only once.*/
		var jsLoadedIndicator=document.createElement("div");
		jsLoadedIndicator.id="grid_openRuleAdvanced_jsLoaded";
		jsLoadedIndicator.style.display="none";
		document.getElementById("pySourceType").parentNode.appendChild(jsLoadedIndicator);
	}
}

"pyActivity":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120548*/,
"pyProperty":"ROWCLASS",

if(!gridFieldPromptingMappings.checkAndUpdatePrompting){
	gridFieldPromptingMappings.checkAndUpdatePrompting=function(fieldObj){
		if(!(document.getElementById("pySourceType") && document.getElementById("pyRowVisible"))){
			return; /*This API is intended only for Repeating Grids, Tree, TreeGrids hence returning from here in other cases. Please do not alter this logic.*/
		}
		if(!fieldObj){return;}
		if(this[fieldObj.id]=="ROWCLASS"){
			if(fieldObj.getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS")){
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(fieldObj.getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			}
		}else if(this[fieldObj.id]=="CUSTOMHANDLING"){
			try{
				GridPropertyPanelActionMappings["handle_"+fieldObj.id]();
				/*Function("GridPropertyPanelActionMappings.handle_"+fieldObj.id+"();")();*/
			}catch(err){
				if(window.console && window.console.log){window.console.log("Error: "+err);}
			}
		}
	};
}

window.GridPropertyPanelActionMappings={
	handle_pyHarnessName:function(){ /*BUG-120593*/ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
	var tmp;
		if((tmp=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass")) && tmp.value==""){
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyHarnessName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pySelectedFlow:function(){ /*BUG-120590*/ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value!=""){
			var pySelectedFlowPromptClass="";
			if(pagesList.length>0 && classesList.length>0){
				for(var q=0;q<pagesList.length;q++){
					if(pagesList[q]==document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value){
						pySelectedFlowPromptClass=classesList[q];
					}
				}
			}
			if(pySelectedFlowPromptClass!=""){
					var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pySelectedFlow").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
					for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
						promptFields[i].value=pySelectedFlowPromptClass;
					}
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
						document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=pySelectedFlowPromptClass;
						fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
					}		
			}
		}else if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value==""){
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pySelectedFlow").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pyActivity:function(){ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyTarget") && document.getElementById("pyTarget")[document.getElementById("pyTarget").selectedIndex].value=="otherSection"){
			this.handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction();
		}else{
			var activityPromptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyActivity").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<activityPromptFields.length;i++){
				activityPromptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pyName:function(){ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyTarget") && document.getElementById("pyTarget")[document.getElementById("pyTarget").selectedIndex].value=="otherSection"){
			this.handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction();
		}else{
			/*BUG-120599: For Report Definition nothing has to be done, but only in case of Open URL in Window (Rule-Obj-Model) some logic is required.*/ 
			/*BUG-120585: Case of Set Value (Rule-Obj-Property) */
			if(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("isns_class")=="Rule-Obj-Model" || document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("isns_class")=="Rule-Obj-Property"){ /*case of Open URL in Window*/
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			}
		}
	},
	handle_pyLocalAction:function(){ /*BUG-120596: Handling Local Action with & without "using page" */ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value==""){ /*without using page -> prompt from row class*/
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyLocalAction").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}
		}else if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value!=""){ /*with using page -> prompt from page class / user entered input class */
			if(!document.getElementById("pyClass") || document.getElementById("pyClass").value==""){
				return;
			}
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyLocalAction").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyClass").value;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=document.getElementById("pyClass").value;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction:function(){ /*Called from within handle_pyActivity, handle_pyName*/
		if(!document.getElementById("pyTarget")){
			return;
		}
		var pyTargetDropDown=document.getElementById("pyTarget");
		var selval=pyTargetDropDown[pyTargetDropDown.selectedIndex].value;
		if(selval=="otherSection"){
			if(document.getElementById("pyActivityClass") && document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value!=""){
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
				}
				var activityPromptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyActivity").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<activityPromptFields.length;i++){
					activityPromptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}		
			}
		}
	}
};

function onChangeHandler(elem, event){
	var evt = window.event || event;
	var srcElement = evt.srcElement || evt.target;
	if(srcElement === elem){
		if(!OpenRuleAdvanced_isActive()) { 
			if(elem.getAttribute("ONCHANGE_CUSTOM") != null) {
				eval(elem.getAttribute("ONCHANGE_CUSTOM"));
			}
			if(elem.getAttribute("ONBLUR_CUSTOM") !=null) {
				eval(elem.getAttribute("ONBLUR_CUSTOM"));
			}
		} 
	}
	else{
		pega.util.Event.fireEvent(elem,'onchange');
		pega.util.Event.fireEvent(elem,'onblur');
	}
}

function fireEventOnField(eventName,fieldObj){
		if(!fieldObj) return;
		if(fieldObj.dispatchEvent){
			var customevent = document.createEvent("HTMLEvents");
			customevent.initEvent(eventName,true,false);
			fieldObj.dispatchEvent(customevent);
		}else if(fieldObj.fireEvent){
			fieldObj.fireEvent("on"+eventName);
		}
}

	}
}

/*Grid related JS code (will be executed only once)*/
if(!document.getElementById("grid_openRuleAdvanced_jsLoaded")){

		var inputList=document.getElementsByTagName("input");
		var pagesList=[];
		var classesList=[];
		for(var i=0;i<inputList.length;i++){
			if(inputList[i].id=="pyPagesAndClassesPage"){
				pagesList.push(inputList[i].value);
			}else if(inputList[i].id=="pyPagesAndClassesClass"){
				classesList.push(inputList[i].value);
			}
		}
		/*END: reading info from pagesAndClassesTab*/
		
		/*reading PRXML from section xml for getting info about PagesAndClasses and Section Parameters*/
		if(document.getElementById("PRXML")){
			var txt=document.getElementById("PRXML").value;
			txt=txt.replace(/\n[ ]*/g, "");
			if(txt.trim){
				txt=txt.trim();
			}
			var cache_prxml=window.cachedPRXML;
			if(!cache_prxml){cache_prxml="";}
			cache_prxml=cache_prxml.replace(/\n[ ]*/g, "");
			if(cache_prxml.trim){
				cache_prxml=cache_prxml.trim();
			}
			var xmlDoc=pega.tools.XMLDocument.get();
			xmlDoc.async= false;
			xmlDoc.loadXML(txt); 
			var xmlDocCache=pega.tools.XMLDocument.get();
			xmlDocCache.async= false;
			xmlDocCache.loadXML(cache_prxml); 
			try{
				gridsectionClassName=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyClassName")[0].text;
			}catch(sectionClassNotFoundError){
				try{
					gridsectionClassName=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyClassName")[0].text;
				}catch(promptClassNotFoundError){

			}
			try{
				gridlRuleSetVersion=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pxInstanceLockedRuleSetVersion")[0].text;

					pagesAndClasses=xmlDocCache.getElementsByTagName("pyPagesAndClasses")[0];
				}
			}catch(err){
			}

				sectionparameters=xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("pyParameters")[0];

			var sourceTypeField=document.getElementById("pySourceType");
			var sourceFieldValue=sourceTypeField[sourceTypeField.selectedIndex].value;
			if(sourceFieldValue=="Property"){
				/*emptying the pyPageListProperty field on UI when the value is .pyTemplatePageList -> when dropping a new grid */
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty") && document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty").value.indexOf("pyTemplatePagelist")!=-1){
					document.getElementById("pyPageListProperty").value="";
				}
				/*Updating the rowpageclass variable*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
			}else if(sourceFieldValue=="Report Definition"){
				/*Update gridrowclass variable*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyRDAppliesTo")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyRDAppliesTo").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
				/*Wait for DOM to be ready after Refresh Section happens.*/
				/*setTimeout(function(){setRDPageDefaults();},1000);*/
			}else if(sourceFieldValue=="Data Object"){
				/*Update rowpageclass*/
				if(document.getElementById("pyDPResultsClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyDPResultsClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass")){
					gridrowPageClassName=document.getElementById("pyPageListPropertyClass").value;
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;}
				}
			}
			/*updating the "PrevValue" with current selection.*/
			document.getElementById("pySourceType").setAttribute("PrevValue",sourceFieldValue);
		}
		/*creating a hidden DOM element to ensure that code is executed only once.*/
		var jsLoadedIndicator=document.createElement("div");
		jsLoadedIndicator.id="grid_openRuleAdvanced_jsLoaded";
		jsLoadedIndicator.style.display="none";
		document.getElementById("pySourceType").parentNode.appendChild(jsLoadedIndicator);
	}
}

var gridFieldPromptingMappings={
"pyActivity":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120548*/,
"pyProperty":"ROWCLASS",
"pyDataSource":"ROWCLASS" /*DISPLAY->MENU*/,
"pyRowRefreshIndex":"ROWCLASS",
"pyActivityClass":"ROWCLASS",
"pySelectedFlowAction":"ROWCLASS" /*PROCESS WORK->PERFORM ACTION*/,
"pyLocalAction":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120596 Launch -> Local Action -> with / without using page */,
"pyWindowName":"ROWCLASS",
"pyValue":"ROWCLASS",
"pyClipboardPage":"ROWCLASS",
"pyWhen":"ROWCLASS",
"pyElementName":"ROWCLASS",
"pyName":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120599, BUG-120548*/,
"pyCategoryHeaderTemplate":"ROWCLASS",
"pyInsName":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120538*/,
"pyInsKey":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120524*/,
"pySelectedFlow":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120590*/,
"pyHarnessName":"CUSTOMHANDLING" /*BUG-120593*/,
"pyKey":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120524*/,
"pyItemId":"ROWCLASS" /*BUG-120524*/
};

if(!gridFieldPromptingMappings.checkAndUpdatePrompting){
	gridFieldPromptingMappings.checkAndUpdatePrompting=function(fieldObj){
		if(!(document.getElementById("pySourceType") && document.getElementById("pyRowVisible"))){
			return; /*This API is intended only for Repeating Grids, Tree, TreeGrids hence returning from here in other cases. Please do not alter this logic.*/
		}
		if(!fieldObj){return;}
		if(this[fieldObj.id]=="ROWCLASS"){
			if(fieldObj.getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS")){
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(fieldObj.getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			}
		}else if(this[fieldObj.id]=="CUSTOMHANDLING"){
			try{
				GridPropertyPanelActionMappings["handle_"+fieldObj.id]();
				/*Function("GridPropertyPanelActionMappings.handle_"+fieldObj.id+"();")();*/
			}catch(err){
				if(window.console && window.console.log){window.console.log("Error: "+err);}
			}
		}
	};
}

window.GridPropertyPanelActionMappings={
	handle_pyHarnessName:function(){ /*BUG-120593*/ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
	var tmp;
		if((tmp=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass")) && tmp.value==""){
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyHarnessName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pySelectedFlow:function(){ /*BUG-120590*/ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value!=""){
			var pySelectedFlowPromptClass="";
			if(pagesList.length>0 && classesList.length>0){
				for(var q=0;q<pagesList.length;q++){
					if(pagesList[q]==document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value){
						pySelectedFlowPromptClass=classesList[q];
					}
				}
			}
			if(pySelectedFlowPromptClass!=""){
					var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pySelectedFlow").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
					for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
						promptFields[i].value=pySelectedFlowPromptClass;
					}
					if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
						document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=pySelectedFlowPromptClass;
						fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
					}		
			}
		}else if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value==""){
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pySelectedFlow").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pyActivity:function(){ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyTarget") && document.getElementById("pyTarget")[document.getElementById("pyTarget").selectedIndex].value=="otherSection"){
			this.handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction();
		}else{
			var activityPromptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyActivity").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<activityPromptFields.length;i++){
				activityPromptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handle_pyName:function(){ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyTarget") && document.getElementById("pyTarget")[document.getElementById("pyTarget").selectedIndex].value=="otherSection"){
			this.handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction();
		}else{
			/*BUG-120599: For Report Definition nothing has to be done, but only in case of Open URL in Window (Rule-Obj-Model) some logic is required.*/ 
			/*BUG-120585: Case of Set Value (Rule-Obj-Property) */
			if(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("isns_class")=="Rule-Obj-Model" || document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("isns_class")=="Rule-Obj-Property"){ /*case of Open URL in Window*/
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}
			}
		}
	},
	handle_pyLocalAction:function(){ /*BUG-120596: Handling Local Action with & without "using page" */ /*Please don't change function name / signature*/
		if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value==""){ /*without using page -> prompt from row class*/
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyLocalAction").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=gridrowPageClassName;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=gridrowPageClassName;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}
		}else if(document.getElementById("pyUsingPage") && document.getElementById("pyUsingPage").value!=""){ /*with using page -> prompt from page class / user entered input class */
			if(!document.getElementById("pyClass") || document.getElementById("pyClass").value==""){
				return;
			}
			var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyLocalAction").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
			for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
				promptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyClass").value;
			}
			if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
				document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=document.getElementById("pyClass").value;
				fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
			}		
		}
	},
	handleOtherSectionScenarioForDisplay_RefreshAction:function(){ /*Called from within handle_pyActivity, handle_pyName*/
		if(!document.getElementById("pyTarget")){
			return;
		}
		var pyTargetDropDown=document.getElementById("pyTarget");
		var selval=pyTargetDropDown[pyTargetDropDown.selectedIndex].value;
		if(selval=="otherSection"){
			if(document.getElementById("pyActivityClass") && document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value!=""){
				var promptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyName").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<promptFields.length;i++){
					promptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
				}
				var activityPromptFields=document.getElementsByName(document.getElementById("pyActivity").getAttribute("ISNS_BASECLASS"));
				for(var i=0;i<activityPromptFields.length;i++){
					activityPromptFields[i].value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
				}
				if(document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass")){
					document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass").value=document.getElementById("pyActivityClass").value;
					fireEventOnField("click",document.getElementById("pySmartPromptClass"));
				}		
			}
		}
	}
};

function onChangeHandler(elem, event){
	var evt = window.event || event;
	var srcElement = evt.srcElement || evt.target;
	if(srcElement === elem){
		if(!OpenRuleAdvanced_isActive()) { 
			if(elem.getAttribute("ONCHANGE_CUSTOM") != null) {
				eval(elem.getAttribute("ONCHANGE_CUSTOM"));
			}
			if(elem.getAttribute("ONBLUR_CUSTOM") !=null) {
				eval(elem.getAttribute("ONBLUR_CUSTOM"));
			}
		} 
	}
	else{
		pega.util.Event.fireEvent(elem,'onchange');
		pega.util.Event.fireEvent(elem,'onblur');
	}
}
</script>

<script>

var pageNameCopy="RH_1";

function updateCustomFields(){
var arDialogArgs = new Array(3);
if (strLockedRuleSet != "") {
		strRuleSet = strLockedRuleSet;
}
if (strLockedRuleSetVersion != "") {
		strRuleSetVersion = strLockedRuleSetVersion ;
}

	
	var objSafeUrl = new SafeURL("@baseclass.ShowXMLOfPage");
	objSafeUrl.put("PageName" , pageNameCopy);
	var strURL = objSafeUrl.toURL();
    var pageXML = httpRequestAsynch(strURL);
	
	var objPageXML = pega.tools.XMLDocument.get();
	objPageXML.async = false;
	objPageXML.loadXML(pageXML);
    
	var customFieldsNode = objPageXML.selectSingleNode("//pyCustomFields");

	if(customFieldsNode != null){	
		var temp = "";
		if(customFieldsNode.selectSingleNode("//pyCFileKey") ==  null){
			temp = "";
			temp = objPageXML.createElement("pyCFileKey");
			customFieldsNode.firstChild.appendChild(temp);
		}
	
		if(customFieldsNode.selectSingleNode("//pyCFieldName") ==  null){
			temp = "";
			temp = objPageXML.createElement("pyCFieldName");
			customFieldsNode.firstChild.appendChild(temp);
		}
		
		if(customFieldsNode.selectSingleNode("//pyCFieldValue") ==  null){
			temp = "";
			temp = objPageXML.createElement("pyCFieldValue");
			customFieldsNode.firstChild.appendChild(temp);
		}

		if(customFieldsNode.selectSingleNode("//pyCFieldType") ==  null){
			temp = "";
			temp = objPageXML.createElement("pyCFieldType");
			customFieldsNode.firstChild.appendChild(temp);
		}
	
		if(customFieldsNode.selectSingleNode("//pyCFileRelativePath") ==  null){
			temp = "";
			temp = objPageXML.createElement("pyCFileRelativePath");
			customFieldsNode.firstChild.appendChild(temp);
		}
	
	}else{
		customFieldsNode = objPageXML.createElement("pyCustomFields");
		customFieldsNode.setAttribute("REPEATINGTYPE","PageGroup");
		
		var rowDataNode = objPageXML.createElement("rowdata");
		rowDataNode.setAttribute("REPEATINGINDEX","empty");			
		customFieldsNode.appendChild(rowDataNode);

		customFieldsNode.firstChild.appendChild(objPageXML.createElement("pyCFileKey"));
		customFieldsNode.firstChild.appendChild(objPageXML.createElement("pyCFieldName"));
		customFieldsNode.firstChild.appendChild(objPageXML.createElement("pyCFieldValue"));
		customFieldsNode.firstChild.appendChild(objPageXML.createElement("pyCFieldType"));
		customFieldsNode.firstChild.appendChild(objPageXML.createElement("pyCFileRelativePath"));
		
		objPageXML.getElementsByTagName("pagedata")[0].appendChild(customFieldsNode);
	}	

	var strCustomFieldsXML = (customFieldsNode != null) ?  customFieldsNode.xml : "";

	arDialogArgs[0] = customFieldsNode;
	arDialogArgs[1] = strCustomFieldsXML;
	arDialogArgs[2] = this;
	 var strUrl = new SafeURL("Embed-CustomFieldsList.showCustomFields");
    strUrl.put("ruleSet", strRuleSet);
    strUrl.put("ruleSetVersion", strRuleSetVersion);
	
	var returnData = showModalDialog(strUrl.toURL(), arDialogArgs, "width:500;height:600;resizable: yes; scroll: no; help: no;");

if (returnData != null) {
		var objReturnData = pega.tools.XMLDocument.get();
		objReturnData.async = false;
		if (!objReturnData.loadXML("<pagedata>" + returnData + "</pagedata>")) {
			alert("bad data returned");
		}
		else {
			var objReturnCustom = objReturnData.documentElement.selectSingleNode("pyCustomFields");
			var theParent = customFieldsNode.parentNode;
			theParent.replaceChild(objReturnCustom, customFieldsNode);
		}
 
		var updatedXML =  "<?xml version=\"1.0\"?>" + theParent.xml;	
		objSafeUrl = new SafeURL("@baseclass.UpdateCustomFieldsInPage");
		objSafeUrl.put("PageName" , pageName);
		strURL = objSafeUrl.toURL();
		var xmlhttp = new ActiveXObject ("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
		xmlhttp.Open("POST", strURL , false);
		xmlhttp.Send(updatedXML);

	}
	var sectionNode = pega.u.d.getSectionByName("RuleFormHistory", null, null);
	pega.u.d.reloadSection(sectionNode, "", "", false, false, "-1", false);
         	//document.getElementById("pyAction~$").click();
}
